Your task is to translate each MathML expression into valid Nemeth braille using only Unicode braille characters. For each MathML input, output ONLY the raw Unicode braille characters. (e.g., '‚†ã‚†∑‚†π‚†Ç‚†å‚†Ü‚†º‚†æ')It is important to pay attention to generating Unicode braille spaces when needed in the braille. It is also important to pay attention when to generate the number sign indicator ‚†º and the English letter indicatorDo not include markdown formatting, explanations, or any other text.Add '|next-item|' between each braille output.
